name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Family Room
info:Stayed in February 2024

posted:Posted February 22, 2024
msg:Cash was lost in the room, and the hotel's attitude in handling the problem was terrible, chilling and angry. It can be said to have ruined our entire trip.
During the Chinese New Year, I took some cash with me and left it in the hotel when I went out. When I came back, I found that the 100 yuan in cash was gone, and I only had a few pieces of change left (Thank you very much, I left a few yuan for a bus trip). Why not put a safe? Sorry, the most luxurious suite in this self-proclaimed five-diamond luxury hotel does not provide a safe. The hotel's attitude towards handling lost money is outrageous:
1. We are not familiar with the place. We asked the hotel if we could help call the police if we needed to. The hotel was unwilling to do so because calling the police might have a bad impact on the hotel‚Äôs reputation (yes, the loss of customers is not important). In fact, we tend not to call the police. We were traveling in a hurry, and there were no cameras in the room to collect evidence. However, the hotel was completely unwilling to provide help, which still made us very disappointed and incomprehensible.
2. So we asked the hotel manager to write down the names of the two waiters who entered our room, thinking that we could call the police ourselves if necessary. The hotel agreed and said that they could not help call the police, but they could provide the name of the waiter.
3. What‚Äôs outrageous is that half an hour later, the hotel manager told us to call the police again. He didn‚Äôt want to give us his name. The reason he gave us was that writing down his name might lead to liability, indicating that the money was stolen by hotel employees. We don't understand the logic at all, but we understand that the hotel just wants to avoid the hotel's responsibility as much as possible, regardless of the guest's thoughts and wishes.
4. It was already ten o'clock at this time. Our family said angrily that we should provide our names first, and we would discuss it before deciding whether to call the police (it was already very late, and we had to go to Huanglong early the next morning). The hotel manager repeatedly said that he should call the police. As soon as he opened the door, six or seven hotel employees were in front of the door. Was there a fight? One of the darker young men yelled at us, "What should we do, what should we do, call the police?" I was shocked at the time. Did we lose money, did the hotel lose money, or did your hotel think that the customer wanted to blackmail you? ? ? We have already rested, and now you are "helping" us to call the police, and are you going to stop letting people rest?
5. It was indeed difficult for the police to collect evidence after they arrived, but they suggested that the hotel should write down the whole story in writing, from when we informed the hotel that the money was lost, to how the hotel handled it, and by checking the surveillance system to find out who had entered and exited our room (this was an explanation for us) ), the hotel manager still kept playing ball. Sometimes he said that the hotel lawyer would not let him, and sometimes he said that the boss would not let him. The police comrades were helpless.
6. I kept writing until after 12 o'clock. After repeated persuasion by the police comrades, the hotel manager agreed to write down what happened to us. He also deceived the police and said that we could leave first, and then he would write it down and bring it to us directly.
7. The next morning we went to the front desk to check out and asked for the written materials promised by the hotel. The waiter who yelled at us before was there and told us that there were no written materials! (Surprise or not, surprise or not)

Throughout the process, we can see that the hotel went back on its word many times for its own benefit, delayed customers' rest regardless of their wishes, and deceived the police and customers. . . The most outrageous thing is that the hotel never said a word of apology from beginning to end!
